	<h1 class="hl ">
						Transform Your Drive</h1>	
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Electricity and gas seamlessly come together to deliver the best of both worlds. It’s electric when you want it, gas when you need it.<br>
</p></div>
				</div>
</div>
</div>
</div></div>
<div class="grid_col1plus2_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pn3a"><div class="section mm_c1"><div class="mds-cmp-content05 mm_1 mod modMm_1" id="">
	<a href="/cars/2014-volt/model-overview/2014-videos.content.html" onclick="if(typeof(Omniture_s) != 'undefined'){mrm.util.tagging.omniture_tl(this, this.href, 'o', undefined, {'prop27':'grid-1+2col'});}" class="btn_lyr"><img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014_Volt/Model_Overview/01_images/2013-Volt-model-overview-technology-cnt-well-1-316X189.png" alt="" width="316" height="189" class="mm"/></a></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3bc">
		<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>With Volt drivers averaging 900 miles between <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_18" class="ln disclaimer_1">fill-ups,<sup>†</sup></a> Volt is continuing to deliver the freedom from the pump.<br>
</p>
<p>The advanced lithium-ion battery first allows you to drive gas-free for an EPA-estimated 38 <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_19" class="ln disclaimer_1">miles.<sup>†</sup></a> Then the onboard gas-powered generator provides electricity so you can drive a total of up to 380 miles on a full charge and full tank of <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_20" class="ln disclaimer_1">gas.<sup>†</sup></a><br>
</p>
<p>With recognition like a number one spot on the Sierra Club’s list of plug-in hybrids and “Leader in Strategic Vision’s 2013 Total Quality Award<sup>TM</sup> for Best Mid-Size Car,”<sup>24</sup> there’s no mistaking that Volt is an everyday electric car that can take you the full distance.</p>
<p>                  No matter how far you need to go, you’re always covered. The Chevrolet 2-Year Scheduled Maintenance coverage<sup>*</sup> includes 4-wheel tire rotation, a 27-point vehicle inspection, oil and oil filter changes and comes standard with the purchase or lease of a 2014 Volt. </p>
<p>Volt is available at participating dealers.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>

									<a href="#" data-link="http://www.chevrolet.com/volt-electric-car.html#" data-picture="http://www.chevrolet.com/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014_Volt/Model_Overview/01_images/2014-chevrolet-volt-model-overview-technology-cnt-well-1-1480x551-03.jpg" data-source="http://www.chevrolet.com/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014_Volt/Model_Overview/01_images/2014-chevrolet-volt-model-overview-technology-cnt-well-1-1480x551-03.jpg" data-name="Chevrolet Volt Technology: Images" data-description="The 2014 Volt is a haven of technology, loaded with Chevrolet MyLink, 7-inch diagonal touchscreen, bluetooth, and more.">
										<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared Resources/01_images/social_share_facebook-16x16.jpg" alt="" width="16" height="16"/></a>
								</li>
							<li class="service-twitter" >
									<a class="icon-twitter" href="https://twitter.com/share?url=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.chevrolet.com%2Fvolt-electric-car.html%23&counturl=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.chevrolet.com%2Fvolt-electric-car.html%23&lang=en&via=chevrolet&related=chevrolet%2Cteamchevy&text=The+2014+%40ChevyVolt+is+a+haven+of+%23technology%2C+with+MyLink%2C++a+7-inch+touchscreen%2C+bluetooth+%26+more%21" target="_blank">

										</li>
							</ul>
			</dd>
		</dl>
	</div>
	<div class="txtWrp">Charging   Volt is easy. Plug it into a 120V electrical outlet using the included   portable charging <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_0" class="ln disclaimer_1">unit<sup>†</sup></a>.</div>

	</div>

<div class="section grid_col1_c1"><div class="mds-area-pf1">
	<div class="pf1a_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					Cutting-Edge Technology</h2>
			</div></div>
</div>
</div></div>
<div class="grid_col2plus1_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3ab">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Charging for about $1.60 per <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_21" class="ln disclaimer_1">day<sup>†</sup></a></h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>For less than the cost of a latte, you can fully charge your Volt and drive an EPA-estimated 38 miles <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_19" class="ln disclaimer_1">gas-free.<sup>†</sup></a> Choose a standard 120V charging <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_22" class="ln disclaimer_1">unit<sup>†</sup></a> that allows you to fully charge the battery in about 10 to 16 <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_9" class="ln disclaimer_1">hours.<sup>†</sup></a> Or opt for an available 240V charging station that cuts down your charging time to approximately four hours. Professional installation required. For more information, visit <a href="http://www.pluginnow.com/go/volt" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('http://www.pluginnow.com/go/volt');" target="_blank">Bosch Automotive Service Solutions.</a></p></div>
		</div>
<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Drive intuitively</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>If you can drive, you can drive a Volt. Instead of turning a key, you push a blue button. Rather than looking at dials and needles, you check two interactive LCD screens for feedback based on four driving modes you can seemlessly switch between to best suit your driving style.</p>
<p>Normal mode enables Volt to drive like a conventional car, only more efficiently. Sport mode gives drivers more aggressive feedback and heightened response. Mountain mode maintains a power reserve for climbing long, steep grades. And Hold mode allows you to hold your battery charge in reserve during stop-and-go traffic.</p>
<p>Even the simple act of braking has been taken to the next level with regenerative braking, which captures some of the energy usually lost during braking and converts it to electricity that’s stored in the battery.</p>
<p><a href="/cars/2014-volt/model-overview/how-the-volt-works.content.html" onclick="if(typeof(Omniture_s) != 'undefined'){mrm.util.tagging.omniture_tl(this, this.href, 'o', undefined, {'prop27':'grid-2+1col'});}" class="btn_lyr">Watch the video to learn How Volt Works.</a></p></div>
		</div>

	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf3a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014_Volt/Model_Overview/01_images/2014-chevrolet-volt-model-overview-technology-cnt-well-1-92x32-07.png" alt="" width="92" height="32" class="img"/><span>
						Chevrolet MyLink</span>
				</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Volt comes with all of the technology you expect from a game changer. Amenities like the Chevrolet <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_23" class="ln disclaimer_1">MyLink™<sup>†</sup></a> Radio with 7-inch diagonal color display touch-screen that lets you easily navigate through an amazing array of information and entertainment options. Bring <a href="http://www.pandora.com/" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('http://www.pandora.com/');" target="_blank">Pandora<sup>®</sup> Internet Radio,</a><sup><a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_35" class="ln disclaimer_1">†</a></sup> Stitcher <a href="http://www.stitcher.com/" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('http://www.stitcher.com/');" target="_blank">SmartRadio™</a><sup><a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_35" class="ln disclaimer_1">†</a></sup> and <a href="http://www.gracenote.com/" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('http://www.gracenote.com/');" target="_blank">Gracenote<sup>®</sup></a><a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_35" class="ln disclaimer_1">†</a> along for the ride.                 Complete an array of hands-free tasks with <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_12" class="ln disclaimer_1">Siri Eyes Free<sup>†</sup></a> when connected through iPhone 4S or iPhone 5.  Chevrolet <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_23" class="ln disclaimer_1">MyLink<sup>†</sup></a> also allows streaming audio content from select smartphones to converge on the color touch-screen display.</p>
<p><a href="/2014-mylink-radio.html" onclick="if(typeof(Omniture_s) != 'undefined'){mrm.util.tagging.omniture_tl(this, this.href, 'o', undefined, {'prop27':'grid-3col'});}">Learn more about MyLink.</a><br>
</p></div>

Volt offers three trial months of <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_25" class="ln disclaimer_1">SiriusXM Satellite Radio<sup>†</sup></a> standard. <a href="http://www.siriusxm.com/" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('http://www.siriusxm.com/');" target="_blank">See channel listings and more info</a>.</p></div>

						Turn-by-turn navigation</span>
				</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">

You can even create a navigation course from MapQuest<sup>®</sup> through eNav™. Simply send that information to your Volt and access those directions on your Chevrolet <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_23" class="ln disclaimer_1">MyLink™<sup>†</sup></a> Radio with 7-inch diagonal color touch-screen when you get in the cockpit.</p></div>

		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>It’s more than an app – it’s a community of Volt owners engaged in friendly competition. You can track the efficiency of your Volt and set goals to maximize it. Then one-up other Volt drivers to earn achievements, scorecards and a spot on the leaderboards. Better yet, it’s all in the name of gallons saved. <a href="/voltdcapp.html" onclick="if(typeof(Omniture_s) != 'undefined'){mrm.util.tagging.omniture_tl(this, this.href, 'o', undefined, {'prop27':'grid-1+2col'});}">Read more</a>.<br>

</p>
<p></p></div>

<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			OnStar RemoteLink™</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Take charge of your battery. The OnStar RemoteLink™ mobile <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_3" class="ln disclaimer_1">app<sup>†</sup></a> shows the battery level and charge mode of your Volt –120V or 240V – right on your smartphone. You’ll be able to remotely verify that your Volt is plugged in, schedule a future charging time and receive charge alerts.&nbsp;Beyond the battery, this app also lets you lock or unlock your doors, or remotely start your Volt from anywhere you get cell service.  <a href="/onstar-remotelink.html" onclick="if(typeof(Omniture_s) != 'undefined'){mrm.util.tagging.omniture_tl(this, this.href, 'o', undefined, {'prop27':'grid-1+2col'});}">Read more</a>.<br>
<br>
Download it now from the <a href="https://itunes.apple.com/us/app/onstar-remotelink/id393584149?mt=8" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('https://itunes.apple.com/us/app/onstar-remotelink/id393584149?mt=8');" target="_blank">App Store</a> or <a href="https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.gm.onstar.mobile.mylink&hl=en" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.gm.onstar.mobile.mylink&hl=en');" target="_blank">Google Play</a>.<br>
</p>
<p>To further connect your Volt through OnStar<sup>®</sup>, go to <a href="https://secure.myvolt.com/web/portal/home" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('https://secure.myvolt.com/web/portal/home');" target="_blank">MyVolt.com</a>.</p>

			<div class="inner" style="width: 980px; top: -180px; margin-bottom: -180px; margin-left: -252px;">
			  <img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014_Volt/Model_Overview/01_images/2014-chevrolet-volt-model-overview-performance-cnt-well-1-1480x264-05.png" alt="" width="1480" height="264" class="mm"/></div>

<div class="grid_col2plus1_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3ab">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Extend your range</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Fully charged, a 16.5 kWh lithium-ion battery powers Volt for an EPA-estimated 38 electric <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_19" class="ln disclaimer_1">miles<sup>†</sup></a>. If you also have a full tank of gas, the total driving range is up to 380 <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_20" class="ln disclaimer_1">miles.<sup>†</sup></a> And if the battery runs low, you don’t have to worry because Volt automatically transitions to a unique gasoline powered range-extending capability. It’s the everyday electric car, with gas for longer trips.</p>
<p>And when it comes to the battery, you always have a backup plan. Chevrolet keeps you covered with a 8-year/100,000-mile Battery and Voltec Component Limited <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_27" class="ln disclaimer_1">Warranty.<sup>†</sup></a></p></div>
		</div>

<div class="grid_col2_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf2">
	<div class="pf2a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			All-over aerodynamic design</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>When it comes to Volt, form and function unite to create a vehicle that’s sporty, quick, smooth and modern, yet achieves an extremely low drag coefficient.</p>
<p>Countless hours in the wind tunnel influenced the styling of many exterior components including mirrors, a closed grille, rocker panels and the rear spoiler. In fact, the vertical blades that go from the bottom of the spoiler to the bottom of the bumper were specifically sculpted to trick the air into separating from the bumper more quickly, giving Volt extraordinary aerodynamics.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf2b">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2b_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Another spin on styling</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Make a smart statement with available 17-inch polished-aluminum wheels. Or opt for available 17-inch sport alloy wheels with black inserts, which come with the option for dealer-installed inserts available in Silver Ice Metallic or Cyber Gray Metallic.</p>
<p>Reduce friction by driving on specialized Goodyear low rolling resistance tires and get up to one additional all-electric mile when compared to ordinary tires.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
</div></div>

</div></div>
<div class="grid_col3_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf3a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Display advanced thinking</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Inside the cockpit you’ll discover new technology that empowers your driving experience like never before. Two interactive color LCD screens allow you to monitor information and get efficiency feedback based on your driving style. You can even set up your Volt to make the most of charging times. If rates are lower at certain times of the day or night, your Volt can be scheduled to charge only when the price is right. Electricity costs vary, so check with your provider for your rates and to determine the best time to charge your Volt.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3b">
		<div class="pf3b_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Innovative space</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Just like the exterior, Volt has an interior with a flow of its own. A unique design incorporates a full center console with sporty bucket seats for four. Cup holders, storage bins, door panel storage, cargo <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_28" class="ln disclaimer_1">space<sup>†</sup></a>—10.6 cubic feet to be exact—all the things you’d expect are there. What you don’t expect is a dedicated umbrella pocket and another storage area for the standard 120V charging cord.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="pf3c_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Select your style</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Volt offers a number of striking interior color combinations. Premium cloth is standard. But you can also opt for available leather-appointed, heated seats in Jet Black with Dark Argent or Ceramic White accents, or select Pebble Beige with sueded inserts and Dark Argent accents. <a href="/volt-electric-car/specs/trims.html" onclick="if(typeof(Omniture_s) != 'undefined'){mrm.util.tagging.omniture_tl(this, this.href, 'o', undefined, {'prop27':'grid-3col'});}">See the complete list of features and specs.</a><br>
</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>

</li><li><div class="cnt_btn_1 mod modCnt_btn_1 section mds-cmp-content02"><a href="/chevy-awards.html#Volt" onclick="if(typeof(Omniture_s) != 'undefined'){mrm.util.tagging.omniture_tl(this, this.href, 'o', undefined, {'prop27':'contentarea'});}" class="btn_sec"><span>See all Volt Awards</span>
		</a></div>
</li></ul></div>
</div>
</div>
</div><div class="mds-area-pf1"><div class="cnt_well_c1 section"><div class="mod modCnt_well_1 mds-cmp-content20" id="Safety">
	<div class="parsys_cnt_well_1 parsys_c1"><div class="section grid_col1_c1"><div class="mds-area-pf1">
	<div class="pf1a_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					A Name In Safety</h2>
			</div></div>
</div>
</div></div>
<div class="grid_col1plus2_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pn3a"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Raising standards</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>When it comes to safety, there’s no mistaking that Volt has raised the bar. The 2013 Volt received a 5-Star Overall Vehicle Score for safety from the National Highway Traffic Safety <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_29" class="ln disclaimer_1">Administration<sup>†</sup></a> and was named a 2013 Top Safety Pick by the Insurance Institute for Highway Safety. When it comes to the latest safety standards, these accolades speak volumes.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3bc">
		<div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05">
			<div class="inner">
	<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014_Volt/Model_Overview/01_images/2014-chevrolet-volt-model-overview-safety-cnt-well-1-340x338-01.jpg" alt="Chevy Volt Safety - Chassis" width="648" height="221" class="mm"/></div>


</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="grid_col1plus2_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pn3a"><div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05 ui_position_float_rel ui_layer_behind">
			<div class="inner" style="width: 980px; top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: -10px;">
			  <img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014_Volt/Model_Overview/01_images/2014-chevrolet-volt-model-overview-safety-cnt-well-1-340x338-02.jpg" alt="" width="340" height="338" class="mm"/></div>


</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3bc">
		<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Cameras, sensors and helpful alerts</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Your drive begins with the aid of an available rear vision camera system that shows what’s behind you when traveling in reverse at low speeds. Rear park assist will audibly alert you of hazards found on the rear vision camera system. Drivers can also activate another audible alert that helps caution pedestrians who may not hear Volt approaching at low speeds.</p>
<p>Avoid or lessen the damage caused by incoming collisions with Forward Collision <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_30" class="ln disclaimer_1">Alert<sup>†</sup></a> which uses a forward-facing camera to alert you of slowing vehicles. There’s also available Lane Departure <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_30" class="ln disclaimer_1">Warning<sup>†</sup></a> that monitors lane markings and warns you in case you are drifting out of their lane.</p>
<p>Lastly, there is the confidence of the StabiliTrak<sup>®</sup> Electronic Stability Control System with Traction Control that is designed to help keep you on your intended course.</p></div>
		</div>
<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Immediately responsive</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>In addition to eight standard air <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_31" class="ln disclaimer_1">bags<sup>†</sup></a> should a collision occur, Volt also automatically relays crucial information to the OnStar® Command Center via OnStar® Automatic Crash <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-volt_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_7" class="ln disclaimer_1">Response.<sup>†</sup></a> There, trained OnStar Advisors utilize GPS technology to pinpoint your exact location and can request that assistance be sent right away—even if you’re unable to respond. OnStar is standard for three years.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

</div><div class="mds-area-pf1"><div class="cnt_well_c1 section"><div class="mod modCnt_well_1 mds-cmp-content20" id="Ecologic">
	<div class="parsys_cnt_well_1 parsys_c1"><div class="grid_col1plus2_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pn3a"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					HOW SUSTAINABLE IS THE VOLT?</h2>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Check out its Ecologic features. Here at Chevrolet, we believe in being a responsible steward of our environment. We’ve developed a way to communicate some of the environmentally significant features of each vehicle we make. We call it Ecologic.</p></div>
				</div></div>
<div class="section mm_c1"><div class="mds-cmp-content05 mm_1 mod modMm_1" id="">
	<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared%20Resources/01_images/2014-chevrolet-model-overview-ecologic-cnt-well-1-308x76-01.jpg" alt="" width="308" height="76" class="mm"/></div>
</div>
<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Every aspect of Ecologic is audited by Two Tomorrows, an independent third-party sustainability auditor. To learn more about Ecologic and the Two Tomorrows process, <a href="/culture/article/ecologic.html" onclick="if(typeof(Omniture_s) != 'undefined'){mrm.util.tagging.omniture_tl(this, this.href, 'o', undefined, {'prop27':'grid-1+2col'});}">click here</a>.<br>
</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3bc">
		<div class="section mm_c1"><div class="mds-cmp-content05 mm_1 mod modMm_1" id="">
	<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared%20Resources/01_images/2014-chevrolet-model-overview-ecologic-cnt-well-1-648x315-02.jpg" alt="" width="648" height="315" class="mm"/></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="grid_col2_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf2">
	<div class="pf2a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Fuel-Saving Technologies</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>                  Volt uses stored electricity initially to propel the vehicle and has a gas-powered range extender that activates when battery power is depleted. When needed, the gas-powered range extender allows the vehicle to travel hundreds of additional miles.</p>
<p>  Regenerative braking recaptures the energy of the car’s forward motion and converts it into electricity. By recycling some of the energy generated from braking, the battery is supplied with recaptured energy without producing additional emissions.</p>
<p>  Low rolling resistance tires reduce the energy needed to keep Volt moving, which improves fuel economy.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf2b">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2b_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Responsible Manufacturing</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>                  The assembly facility features one of the largest photovoltaic solar arrays in Southeast Michigan at 516 kilowatts. This renewable energy conserves resources and reduces dependence on fossil fuels.</p>
<p>  The engine, transmission and battery facilities are landfill-free. These facilities use a process to reuse, recycle or convert to energy all waste created in their daily operations, which conserves resources.</p></div>
		</div>
<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			End-of-Life Recyclability</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>                  After the vehicle’s useful life, 85% of it is recyclable. The majority of its components can be broken down and recycled, which conserves resources and reduces landfill deposits.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
